      <div class="fl-row fl-row-fixed-width fl-row-bg-none fl-node-586ff94adedac intro-wrapper-with-image" data-node="586ff94adedac">
       <div class="fl-row-content-wrap">
        <div class="fl-row-content fl-row-fixed-width fl-node-content">
         <div class="fl-col-group fl-node-586ff94adebff fl-col-group-equal-height fl-col-group-align-center" data-node="586ff94adebff">
          <div class="fl-col fl-node-586ff94adec4e" data-node="586ff94adec4e">
           <div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content">
            <div class="fl-module fl-module-photo fl-node-586ff94adecd9" data-node="586ff94adecd9" id="welcome-img">
             <div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
              <div class="fl-photo fl-photo-align-center" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
               <div class="fl-photo-content fl-photo-img-jpg">
                <img alt="Forest ranger on Cabinet National Forest, Montana, 1909." class="fl-photo-img wp-image-19 size-full" height="482" itemprop="image" sizes="(max-width: 633px) 100vw, 633px" src="https://foresthistory.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/intro-image.jpg" srcset="https://foresthistory.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/intro-image.jpg 633w, https://foresthistory.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/intro-image-300x228.jpg 300w, https://foresthistory.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/intro-image-500x381.jpg 500w" title="intro-image" width="633"/>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="fl-col fl-node-586ff94adec94 fl-col-small" data-node="586ff94adec94">
           <div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content">
            <div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-586ff94aded1f mobile-space" data-node="586ff94aded1f" id="welcome-text">
             <div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
              <div class="fl-rich-text">
               <h2>
                Welcome
               </h2>
               <p>
                The Forest History Society is a nonprofit library and archive dedicated to collecting, preserving, and disseminating forest and conservation history for all to use. The Society links the past to the future while reminding us about our important forest heritage.
               </p>
               <p>
                As part of our mission, FHS is continually seeking innovative ways of enhancing its programs in research, publication, and education, and new methods for promoting the study of environmental history. Towards that end, you'll now find us on Facebook and Twitter and blogging at Peeling Back the Bark. We invite you to take a tour of FHS, and then explore the website and discover your forest heritage!
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="fl-module fl-module-button fl-node-58b827439a089 more mobile-space" data-node="58b827439a089">
             <div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
              <div class="fl-button-wrap fl-button-width-auto fl-button-left">
               <a class="fl-button" href="https://foresthistory.org/about/" role="button" target="_self">
                <span class="fl-button-text">
                 Learn More
                </span>
               </a>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>

              <div class="fl-rich-text">
               <h2 style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="color: #ffffff;">
                 RESEARCH &amp; EXPLORE
                </span>
               </h2>
               <p style="text-align: center;">
                <span style="color: #ffffff;">
                 Our Library and Archives contain an extensive collection of published works, photographs, and primary sources that provide a comprehensive look at forest, conservation, and environmental history.
                </span>
               </p>

   <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

$( ".soliloquy-caption-bottom .soliloquy-caption-inside" ).wrapInner( "<div id='slider-title'><div id='slider-cell'></div></div>");

myBlurFunction = function(state) {

    /* state can be 1 or 0 */

    var containerElement = document.getElementById('main_container');

    var overlayEle = document.getElementById('searchOverlay');



    if (state) {

       

        containerElement.setAttribute('class', 'blur');

    } else {

      

        containerElement.setAttribute('class', null);

    }

};

  

jQuery(document).ready(function($) {  

    $('li.bodyToggle').on('click', function() {
		$("#main_container").addClass("blur")

      $('body').addClass("noScroll");

	  $('#searchOverlay').fadeIn(300);

    });

	

	$('a.bodyToggle2').on('click', function() {
		$("#main_container").removeClass("blur")

      $('body').removeClass("noScroll");

	  $('#searchOverlay').fadeOut(300);

    });

	

	

	$('a.slicknav_btn').on('click', function() {

      $('.slicknav_menu').toggleClass("height");

	  $('body').toggleClass("noScroll");

    });
	

	

});	

		if (window.matchMedia("(max-width: 900px)").matches) {
    $("body .envirabox-skin.envirabox-theme-captioned .envirabox-title-float-wrap span.child").append("div class='mobile-slide'></div>");
}
   </script>
